I've uploaded a code repository in the directory /testbed. Consider the following PR description:

<pr_description>
minifier: inlining variables in object when string key is encountered
i noticed a bug with logic used to inline variables, that is present only when object with property of type string is present before variable that should be inlined

```ts
var o = "test-b", l = {
	"test-a": "test-a",
	testb: o,
};
export { l };
/// out
var o = "test-b", l = {
	"test-a": "test-a",
	testb: o
};
export { l };
```
[play](https://playground.oxc.rs/?options=%7B%22run%22%3A%7B%22lint%22%3Atrue%2C%22formatter%22%3Afalse%2C%22transform%22%3Afalse%2C%22isolatedDeclarations%22%3Afalse%2C%22whitespace%22%3Afalse%2C%22mangle%22%3Afalse%2C%22compress%22%3Atrue%2C%22scope%22%3Atrue%2C%22symbol%22%3Atrue%2C%22cfg%22%3Afalse%7D%2C%22parser%22%3A%7B%22extension%22%3A%22tsx%22%2C%22allowReturnOutsideFunction%22%3Atrue%2C%22preserveParens%22%3Atrue%2C%22allowV8Intrinsics%22%3Atrue%2C%22semanticErrors%22%3Atrue%7D%2C%22linter%22%3A%7B%7D%2C%22formatter%22%3A%7B%22useTabs%22%3Afalse%2C%22tabWidth%22%3A2%2C%22endOfLine%22%3A%22lf%22%2C%22printWidth%22%3A80%2C%22singleQuote%22%3Afalse%2C%22jsxSingleQuote%22%3Afalse%2C%22quoteProps%22%3A%22as-needed%22%2C%22trailingComma%22%3A%22all%22%2C%22semi%22%3Atrue%2C%22arrowParens%22%3A%22always%22%2C%22bracketSpacing%22%3Atrue%2C%22bracketSameLine%22%3Afalse%2C%22objectWrap%22%3A%22preserve%22%2C%22singleAttributePerLine%22%3Afalse%7D%2C%22transformer%22%3A%7B%22target%22%3A%22es2015%22%2C%22useDefineForClassFields%22%3Atrue%2C%22experimentalDecorators%22%3Atrue%2C%22emitDecoratorMetadata%22%3Atrue%7D%2C%22isolatedDeclarations%22%3A%7B%22stripInternal%22%3Afalse%7D%2C%22codegen%22%3A%7B%22normal%22%3Atrue%2C%22jsdoc%22%3Atrue%2C%22annotation%22%3Atrue%2C%22legal%22%3Atrue%7D%2C%22compress%22%3A%7B%7D%2C%22mangle%22%3A%7B%22topLevel%22%3Atrue%2C%22keepNames%22%3Afalse%7D%2C%22controlFlow%22%3A%7B%22verbose%22%3Afalse%7D%2C%22inject%22%3A%7B%22inject%22%3A%7B%7D%7D%2C%22define%22%3A%7B%22define%22%3A%7B%7D%7D%7D&code=var+o+%3D+%22test-b%22%2C+l+%3D+%7B%0A%09%22test-a%22%3A+%22string%22%2C%0A%09testb%3A+o%2C%0A%7D%3B%0Aexport+%7B+l+%7D%3B)

this issue is present only when `"test-a"` string is enoutered and it works correctly when `"` can be removed
```ts
var o = "test-b", l = {
	"testa": "test-a",
	testb: o,
};
export { l };
//// out
var l = {
	testa: "test-a",
	testb: "test-b"
};
export { l };
```

</pr_description>

    12	        let BindingPattern::BindingIdentifier(ident) = &decl.id else { return };
    13	        let Some(symbol_id) = ident.symbol_id.get() else { return };
    14	        let value = if decl.kind.is_var() || Self::is_for_statement_init(ctx) {

   205	    pub fn is_expression_undefined(&self, expr: &Expression) -> bool {
   206	        match expr {
   207	            Expression::Identifier(ident) if self.is_identifier_undefined(ident) => true,
   208	            Expression::UnaryExpression(e) if e.operator.is_void() && e.argument.is_number() => {
   209	                true
   210	            }
   211	            _ => false,
   212	        }
   213	    }
   214	
   215	    #[inline]
   216	    pub fn is_identifier_undefined(&self, ident: &IdentifierReference) -> bool {
   217	        if ident.name == "undefined" && ident.is_global_reference(self.scoping()) {
   218	            return true;
   219	        }
   220	        false
   221	    }
   222	
   223	    pub fn init_value(&mut self, symbol_id: SymbolId, constant: Option<ConstantValue<'a>>) {
   224	        let mut exported = false;
   225	        if self.scoping.current_scope_id() == self.scoping().root_scope_id() {
   226	            for ancestor in self.ancestors() {
   227	                if ancestor.is_export_named_declaration()
   228	                    || ancestor.is_export_all_declaration()
   229	                    || ancestor.is_export_default_declaration()
   230	                {
   231	                    exported = true;
   232	                }
   233	            }
   234	        }
   235	
   236	        let mut read_references_count = 0;
   237	        let mut write_references_count = 0;
   238	        for r in self.scoping().get_resolved_references(symbol_id) {
   239	            if r.is_read() {
   240	                read_references_count += 1;
   241	            }
   242	            if r.is_write() {
   243	                write_references_count += 1;
   244	            }
   245	        }
   246	
   247	        let scope_id = self.scoping().symbol_scope_id(symbol_id);
   248	        let scope_flags = self.scoping().scope_flags(scope_id);
   249	
   250	        let initialized_constant =
   251	            if scope_flags.contains(ScopeFlags::DirectEval) { None } else { constant };
   252	
   253	        let symbol_value = SymbolValue {
   254	            initialized_constant,
   255	            exported,
   256	            read_references_count,
   257	            write_references_count,
   258	            scope_id,
   259	        };
   260	        self.state.symbol_values.init_value(symbol_id, symbol_value);
   261	    }
   262	
   263	    /// If two expressions are equal.
   264	    /// Special case `undefined` == `void 0`
   265	    pub fn expr_eq(&self, a: &Expression<'a>, b: &Expression<'a>) -> bool {
   266	        use oxc_span::ContentEq;
   267	        a.content_eq(b) || (self.is_expression_undefined(a) && self.is_expression_undefined(b))
   268	    }

  1204	    fn substitute_single_use_symbol_within_declaration(
  1205	        kind: VariableDeclarationKind,
  1206	        declarations: &mut Vec<'a, VariableDeclarator<'a>>,
  1207	        ctx: &TraverseCtx<'a>,
  1208	    ) -> bool {
  1209	        if Self::keep_top_level_var_in_script_mode(ctx)
  1210	            || ctx.current_scope_flags().contains_direct_eval()

  1212	        {
  1213	            return false;
  1214	        }
  1215	
  1216	        let mut changed = false;
  1217	        let mut i = 1;
  1218	        while i < declarations.len() {
  1219	            let (prev_decls, [decl, ..]) = declarations.split_at_mut(i) else { unreachable!() };
  1220	            let Some(decl_init) = &mut decl.init else {

  1232	                i -= drop_count;

  1272	            let replaced = Self::substitute_single_use_symbol_in_expression(
  1273	                target_expr,
  1274	                &prev_decl_id.name,
  1275	                prev_decl_init,
  1276	                prev_decl_init.may_have_side_effects(ctx),
  1277	                ctx,
  1278	            );
  1279	            if replaced != Some(true) {
  1280	                return true;
  1281	            }
  1282	            false
  1283	        });
  1284	        match last_non_inlined_index {
  1285	            None => 0,
  1286	            Some(last_non_inlined_index) => last_non_inlined_index + 1,
  1287	        }
  1288	    }
  1289	
  1290	    /// Returns Some(true) when the expression is successfully replaced.
  1291	    /// Returns Some(false) when the expression is not replaced, and cannot try the subsequent expressions.
  1292	    /// Return None when the expression is not replaced, and can try the subsequent expressions.
  1293	    ///
  1294	    /// `substituteSingleUseSymbolInExpr`: <https://github.com/evanw/esbuild/blob/v0.25.9/internal/js_parser/js_parser.go#L9642>
  1295	    fn substitute_single_use_symbol_in_expression(
  1296	        target_expr: &mut Expression<'a>,
  1297	        search_for: &str,
  1298	        replacement: &mut Expression<'a>,
  1299	        replacement_has_side_effect: bool,
  1300	        ctx: &TraverseCtx<'a>,
  1301	    ) -> Option<bool> {
  1302	        match target_expr {
  1303	            Expression::Identifier(id) => {
  1304	                if id.name == search_for {
  1305	                    *target_expr = replacement.take_in(ctx.ast);
  1306	                    return Some(true);
  1307	                }
  1308	                // If the identifier is not a getter and the identifier is read-only,
  1309	                // we know that the value is same even if we reordered the expression.
  1310	                if let Some(symbol_id) = ctx.scoping().get_reference(id.reference_id()).symbol_id()
  1311	                    && !ctx.scoping().symbol_is_mutated(symbol_id)
  1312	                {
  1313	                    return None;
  1314	                }
  1315	            }
  1316	            Expression::AwaitExpression(await_expr) => {
  1317	                if let Some(changed) = Self::substitute_single_use_symbol_in_expression(
  1318	                    &mut await_expr.argument,
  1319	                    search_for,
  1320	                    replacement,
  1321	                    replacement_has_side_effect,
  1322	                    ctx,
  1323	                ) {
  1324	                    return Some(changed);
  1325	                }
  1326	            }
  1327	            Expression::YieldExpression(yield_expr) => {
  1328	                if let Some(argument) = &mut yield_expr.argument
  1329	                    && let Some(changed) = Self::substitute_single_use_symbol_in_expression(
  1330	                        argument,
  1331	                        search_for,
  1332	                        replacement,
  1333	                        replacement_has_side_effect,
  1334	                        ctx,
  1335	                    )

  1685	                        }
  1686	                    }
  1687	                }
  1688	            }
  1689	            Expression::ArrayExpression(array_expr) => {

  1747	                                }

  1842	        // effects, then we can reorder the replacement past this expression
  1843	        //
  1844	        // ```js
  1845	        // // Substitution is ok
  1846	        // let replacement = 123;
  1847	        // return x + replacement;
  1848	        //
  1849	        // // Substitution is not ok because "fn()" may change "x"

  1851	        // return x + replacement;
  1852	        //

  1854	        // let replacement = [x];
  1855	        // return (x == x) + replacement;
  1856	        // ```
  1857	        if !replacement_has_side_effect && !target_expr.may_have_side_effects(ctx) {
